--></mo>\n<mrow>\n<mo>(</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mi>z</mi>\n<msqrt>\n<mn>2</mn>\n</msqrt>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo>)</mo>\n</mrow>\n</mrow>\n<mo>]</mo>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\text{Proportion}}\\leq x={\\frac {1}{2}}\\left[1+\\operatorname {erf} \\left({\\frac {x-\\mu }{\\sigma {\\sqrt {2}}}}\\right)\\right]={\\frac {1}{2}}\\left[1+\\operatorname {erf} \\left({\\frac {z}{\\sqrt {2}}}\\right)\\right]}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle {\\text{Proportion}}\\leq x={\\frac {1}{2}}\\left[1+\\operatorname {erf} \\left({\\frac {x-\\mu }{\\sigma {\\sqrt {2}}}}\\right)\\right]={\\frac {1}{2}}\\left[1+\\operatorname {erf} \\left({\\frac {z}{\\sqrt {2}}}\\right)\\right]}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3907d1b0502235fa3fd00f261b290406a02e7b21" style="vertical-align: -2.838ex; width:61.839ex; height:6.509ex;"/></span>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></dd></dl>\n<p>If a data distribution is approximately normal then about 68 percent of the data values are within one standard deviation of the mean (mathematically, <i>&#956;</i>&#160;&#177;&#160;<i>&#963;</i>, where <i>&#956;</i> is the arithmetic mean), about 95 percent are within two standard deviations (<i>&#956;</i>&#160;&#177;&#160;2<i>&#963;</i>), and about 99.7 percent lie within three standard deviations (<i>&#956;</i>&#160;&#177;&#160;3<i>&#963;</i>). This is known as the <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/68-95-99.7_rule" title="68-95-99.7 rule">68-95-99.7 rule</a></i>, or <i>the empirical rule</i>.\n</p><p>For various values of <i>z</i>, the percentage of values expected to lie in and outside the symmetric interval, CI&#160;=&#160;(&#8722;<i>z&#963;</i>,&#160;<i>z&#963;</i>), are as follows:\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div within(<i>z</i>)</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Standard_deviation_by_Confidence_interval.svg"><img alt="" style="margin-left:.25em;">256</span></span>%\n</td>\n<td>1&#160;/&#160;<span class="nowrap"><span class="sortkey" style="display:none">7011390682215445000&#9824;</span>390<span style="margin-left:.25em;">682</span><span style="margin-left:.25em;">215</span><span style="margin-left:.25em;">445</span></span>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationship_between_standard_deviation_and_mean">Relationship between standard deviation and mean</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Standard_deviation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Relationship between standard deviation and mean">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The mean and the standard deviation of a set of data are <a href="/wiki/Descriptive_statistics" title="Descriptive statistics">descriptive statistics</a> usually reported together. In a certain sense, the standard deviation is a "natural" measure of <a href="/wiki/Statistical_dispersion" title="Statistical dispersion">statistical dispersion</a> if the center of the data is measured about the mean. This is because the standard deviation from the mean is smaller than from any other point. The precise statement is the following: suppose <i>x</i><sub>1</sub>, ..., <i>x</i><sub><i>n</i></sub> are real numbers and define the function:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma (r)={\\sqrt {{\\frac {1}{N-1}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}(x_{i}-r)^{2}}}.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<mi>r</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mrow>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<munderover>\n<mo>&#8721;<!-- &#8721; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>i</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mrow>\n</munderover>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>x</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>i</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mi>r</mi>\n<msup>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msup>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n<mo>.</mo>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma (r)={\\sqrt {{\\frac {1}{N-1}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}(x_{i}-r)^{2}}}.}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma (r)={\\sqrt {{\\frac {1}{N-1}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}(x_{i}-r)^{2}}}." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/859729efa7b2601d6f46bce346c25ba8061fc16d" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:29.913ex; height:8.009ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Using <a href="/wiki/Calculus" title="Calculus">calculus</a> or by <a href="/wiki/Completing_the_square" title="Completing the square">completing the square</a>, it is possible to show that <i>&#963;</i>(<i>r</i>) has a unique minimum at the mean:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle r={\\overline {x}}.\\,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>r</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mover>\n<mi>x</mi>\n<mo accent="false">&#175;<!-- &#175; --></mo>\n</mover>\n</mrow>\n<mo>.</mo>\n<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle r={\\overline {x}}.\\,}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="r={\\overline {x}}.\\," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/76f600dd5a4d354fffe87b5a2cf79a8a715a42fa" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.626ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Variability can also be measured by the <a href="/wiki/Coefficient_of_variation" title="Coefficient of variation">coefficient of variation</a>, which is the ratio of the standard deviation to the mean.  It is a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dimensionless_number" title="Dimensionless number">dimensionless number</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Standard_deviation_of_the_mean">Standard deviation of the mean</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Standard_deviation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Standard deviation of the mean">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Standard_error_of_the_mean" title="Standard error of the mean">Standard error of the mean</a></div>\n<p>Often, we want some information about the precision of the mean we obtained. We can obtain this by determining the standard deviation of the sampled mean.\nAssuming statistical independence of the values in the sample, the standard deviation of the mean is related to the standard deviation of the distribution by:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{\\text{mean}}={\\frac {1}{\\sqrt {N}}}\\sigma }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtext>mean</mtext>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<msqrt>\n<mi>N</mi>\n</msqrt>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{\\text{mean}}={\\frac {1}{\\sqrt {N}}}\\sigma }</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma _{\\text{mean}}={\\frac {1}{\\sqrt {N}}}\\sigma " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/89bbeee80b569c63f6fe6a773055267ea7b60509" style="vertical-align: -2.838ex; width:14.658ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>where <i>N</i> is the number of observations in the sample used to estimate the mean. This can easily be proven with (see <a href="/wiki/Variance#Basic_properties" title="Variance">basic properties of the variance</a>):\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} (X)&amp;\\equiv \\sigma _{X}^{2}\\\\\\operatorname {var} (X_{1}+X_{2})&amp;\\equiv \\operatorname {var} (X_{1})+\\operatorname {var} (X_{2})\\\\\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>&#8801;<!-- &#8801; --></mo>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>X</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>+</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>&#8801;<!-- &#8801; --></mo>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n<mo>+</mo>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n</mtable>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} (X)&amp;\\equiv \\sigma _{X}^{2}\\\\\\operatorname {var} (X_{1}+X_{2})&amp;\\equiv \\operatorname {var} (X_{1})+\\operatorname {var} (X_{2})\\\\\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} (X)&amp;\\equiv \\sigma _{X}^{2}\\\\\\operatorname {var} (X_{1}+X_{2})&amp;\\equiv \\operatorname {var} (X_{1})+\\operatorname {var} (X_{2})\\\\\\end{aligned}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9c40adbbd83e81cd57ba95350f42d175b7ec45dc" style="vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:36.777ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>(Statistical Independence is assumed.)\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} (cX_{1})&amp;\\equiv c^{2}\\,\\operatorname {var} (X_{1})\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<mi>c</mi>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>&#8801;<!-- &#8801; --></mo>\n<msup>\n<mi>c</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msup>\n<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n</mtable>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} (cX_{1})&amp;\\equiv c^{2}\\,\\operatorname {var} (X_{1})\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} (cX_{1})&amp;\\equiv c^{2}\\,\\operatorname {var} (X_{1})\\end{aligned}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9d5ac137637b2f49d5da1ba6c142f4847bdee0f3" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:23.871ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>hence\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} ({\\text{mean}})&amp;=\\operatorname {var} \\left({\\frac {1}{N}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}X_{i}\\right)={\\frac {1}{N^{2}}}\\operatorname {var} \\left(\\sum _{i=1}^{N}X_{i}\\right)\\\\&amp;={\\frac {1}{N^{2}}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}\\operatorname {var} (X_{i})={\\frac {N}{N^{2}}}\\operatorname {var} (X)={\\frac {1}{N}}\\operatorname {var} (X).\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtext>mean</mtext>\n</mrow>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mrow>\n<mo>(</mo>\n<mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<munderover>\n<mo>&#8721;<!-- &#8721; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>i</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mrow>\n</munderover>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>i</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mrow>\n<mo>)</mo>\n</mrow>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<msup>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msup>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mrow>\n<mo>(</mo>\n<mrow>\n<munderover>\n<mo>&#8721;<!-- &#8721; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>i</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mrow>\n</munderover>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>i</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mrow>\n<mo>)</mo>\n</mrow>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n<mtr>\n<mtd></mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<msup>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msup>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<munderover>\n<mo>&#8721;<!-- &#8721; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>i</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mrow>\n</munderover>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>i</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<msup>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msup>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mi>var</mi>\n<mo>&#8289;<!-- &#8289; --></mo>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<mi>X</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n<mo>.</mo>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n</mtable>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} ({\\text{mean}})&amp;=\\operatorname {var} \\left({\\frac {1}{N}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}X_{i}\\right)={\\frac {1}{N^{2}}}\\operatorname {var} \\left(\\sum _{i=1}^{N}X_{i}\\right)\\\\&amp;={\\frac {1}{N^{2}}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}\\operatorname {var} (X_{i})={\\frac {N}{N^{2}}}\\operatorname {var} (X)={\\frac {1}{N}}\\operatorname {var} (X).\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\begin{aligned}\\operatorname {var} ({\\text{mean}})&amp;=\\operatorname {var} \\left({\\frac {1}{N}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}X_{i}\\right)={\\frac {1}{N^{2}}}\\operatorname {var} \\left(\\sum _{i=1}^{N}X_{i}\\right)\\\\&amp;={\\frac {1}{N^{2}}}\\sum _{i=1}^{N}\\operatorname {var} (X_{i})={\\frac {N}{N^{2}}}\\operatorname {var} (X)={\\frac {1}{N}}\\operatorname {var} (X).\\end{aligned}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b0419885b09d9d4523ac2ac10293c9dd8d1e69b7" style="vertical-align: -6.838ex; width:59.074ex; height:14.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Resulting in:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{\\text{mean}}={\\frac {\\sigma }{\\sqrt {N}}}.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtext>mean</mtext>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<msqrt>\n<mi>N</mi>\n</msqrt>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo>.</mo>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{\\text{mean}}={\\frac {\\sigma }{\\sqrt {N}}}.}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma _{\\text{mean}}={\\frac {\\sigma }{\\sqrt {N}}}." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/89df028af1a042901a16b631764dcfc3c6da6f05" style="vertical-align: -2.838ex; width:13.975ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>It should be emphasized that in order to estimate the standard deviation of the mean <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{\\text{mean}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msub>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtext>mean</mtext>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{\\text{mean}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma _{\\text{mean}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/37e04d0b7e0d823e342f598220a3e355849e8e23" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:5.394ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span> it is necessary to know the standard deviation of the entire population <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma }</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/59f59b7c3e6fdb1d0365a494b81fb9a696138c36" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span> beforehand. However, in most applications this parameter is unknown. For example, if a series of 10 measurements of a previously unknown quantity is performed in a laboratory, it is possible to calculate the resulting sample mean and sample standard deviation, but it is impossible to calculate the standard deviation of the mean.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rapid_calculation_methods">Rapid calculation methods</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Standard_deviation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Rapid calculation methods">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/Algorithms_for_calculating_variance" title="Algorithms for calculating variance">Algorithms for calculating variance</a></div>\n<p>The following two formulas can represent a running (repeatedly updated) standard deviation. A set of two power sums <i>s</i><sub>1</sub> and <i>s</i><sub>2</sub> are computed over a set of <i>N</i> values of <i>x</i>, denoted as <i>x</i><sub>1</sub>, ..., <i>x</i><sub><i>N</i></sub>:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\ s_{j}=\\sum _{k=1}^{N}{x_{k}^{j}}.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mtext>&#160;</mtext>\n<msub>\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>j</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<munderover>\n<mo>&#8721;<!-- &#8721; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mrow>\n</munderover>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msubsup>\n<mi>x</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>j</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n</mrow>\n<mo>.</mo>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\ s_{j}=\\sum _{k=1}^{N}{x_{k}^{j}}.}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\ s_{j}=\\sum _{k=1}^{N}{x_{k}^{j}}." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/312ea68655a22acac5bcbf49f6394df4fef39fda" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:12.487ex; height:7.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Given the results of these running summations, the values <i>N</i>, <i>s</i><sub>1</sub>, <i>s</i><sub>2</sub> can be used at any time to compute the <i>current</i> value of the running standard deviation:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma ={\\frac {\\sqrt {Ns_{2}-s_{1}^{2}}}{N}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<msqrt>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<msub>\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n</msqrt>\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma ={\\frac {\\sqrt {Ns_{2}-s_{1}^{2}}}{N}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma ={\\frac {\\sqrt {Ns_{2}-s_{1}^{2}}}{N}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d4f05d4b068900457715e97a4b859cf7b4af1283" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:16.781ex; height:7.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Where N, as mentioned above, is the size of the set of values (or can also be regarded as <i>s</i><sub>0</sub>).\n</p><p>Similarly for sample standard deviation,\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle s={\\sqrt {\\frac {Ns_{2}-s_{1}^{2}}{N(N-1)}}}.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msqrt>\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<msub>\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n</mrow>\n<mrow>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<mi>N</mi>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</msqrt>\n</mrow>\n<mo>.</mo>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle s={\\sqrt {\\frac {Ns_{2}-s_{1}^{2}}{N(N-1)}}}.}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="s={\\sqrt {\\frac {Ns_{2}-s_{1}^{2}}{N(N-1)}}}." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6f0383a0ab52653ebcf7a2379df4d3fb588669a6" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:17.935ex; height:7.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>In a computer implementation, as the three <i>s</i><sub><i>j</i></sub> sums become large, we need to consider <a href="/wiki/Round-off_error" title="Round-off error">round-off error</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arithmetic_overflow" title="Arithmetic overflow">arithmetic overflow</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Arithmetic_underflow" title="Arithmetic underflow">arithmetic underflow</a>. The method below calculates the running sums method with reduced rounding errors.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup> This is a "one pass" algorithm for calculating variance of <i>n</i> samples without the need to store prior data during the calculation. Applying this method to a time series will result in successive values of standard deviation corresponding to <i>n</i> data points as <i>n</i> grows larger with each new sample, rather than a constant-width sliding window calculation.\n</p><p>For <i>k</i> = 1, ..., <i>n</i>:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}A_{0}&amp;=0\\\\A_{k}&amp;=A_{k-1}+{\\frac {x_{k}-A_{k-1}}{k}}\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<msub>\n<mi>A</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<msub>\n<mi>A</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>A</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>+</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>x</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>A</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mrow>\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n</mtable>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}A_{0}&amp;=0\\\\A_{k}&amp;=A_{k-1}+{\\frac {x_{k}-A_{k-1}}{k}}\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\begin{aligned}A_{0}&amp;=0\\\\A_{k}&amp;=A_{k-1}+{\\frac {x_{k}-A_{k-1}}{k}}\\end{aligned}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0855aebe6c22c37d63d2f1b9b830a1ecccd5bcb6" style="vertical-align: -3.671ex; width:25.482ex; height:8.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>where A is the mean value.\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}Q_{0}&amp;=0\\\\Q_{k}&amp;=Q_{k-1}+{\\frac {k-1}{k}}(x_{k}-A_{k-1})^{2}=Q_{k-1}+(x_{k}-A_{k-1})(x_{k}-A_{k})\\\\\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<msub>\n<mi>Q</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<msub>\n<mi>Q</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>Q</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; width:8.28ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>\n</p><p>Sample variance:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle s_{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{n-1}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msubsup>\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<msub>\n<mi>Q</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mrow>\n<mi>n</mi>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle s_{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{n-1}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="s_{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{n-1}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a773eb1cc191dff65d7bc352b7497bfd8c3e5946" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:11.641ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>Population variance:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{n}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msubsup>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<msub>\n<mi>Q</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{n}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma _{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/71e8caf09fb7416d22fc3d523d1ce3a1176bf985" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:9.537ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weighted_calculation">Weighted calculation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Standard_deviation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Weighted calculation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>When the values <i>x<sub>i</sub></i> are weighted with unequal weights <i>w<sub>i</sub></i>, the power sums <i>s</i><sub>0</sub>, <i>s</i><sub>1</sub>, <i>s</i><sub>2</sub> are each computed as:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\ s_{j}=\\sum _{k=1}^{N}{w_{k}x_{k}^{j}}.\\,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mtext>&#160;</mtext>\n<msub>\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>j</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<munderover>\n<mo>&#8721;<!-- &#8721; --></mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>N</mi>\n</mrow>\n</munderover>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<msub>\n<mi>w</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>x</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>j</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n</mrow>\n<mo>.</mo>\n<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\ s_{j}=\\sum _{k=1}^{N}{w_{k}x_{k}^{j}}.\\,}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\ s_{j}=\\sum _{k=1}^{N}{w_{k}x_{k}^{j}}.\\," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/27d71e34e39189b97eac592b9970cfbfe5c59e89" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:15.627ex; height:7.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>And the standard deviation equations remain unchanged.  Note that <i>s</i><sub>0</sub> is now the sum of the weights and not the number of samples <i>N</i>.\n</p><p>The incremental method with reduced rounding errors can also be applied, with some additional complexity.\n</p><p>A running sum of weights must be computed for each <i>k</i> from 1 to <i>n</i>:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}W_{0}&amp;=0\\\\W_{k}&amp;=W_{k-1}+w_{k}\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<msub>\n<mi>W</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<msub>\n<mi>W</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>W</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>+</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>w</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n</mtable>\n</mrow>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}W_{0}&amp;=0\\\\W_{k}&amp;=W_{k-1}+w_{k}\\end{aligned}}}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\begin{aligned}W_{0}&amp;=0\\\\W_{k}&amp;=W_{k-1}+w_{k}\\end{aligned}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/901b1526fb01008c6c137266656c5ff5fef783e7" style="vertical-align: -2.1ex; margin-bottom: -0.238ex; width:18.109ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>and places where 1/<i>n</i> is used above must be replaced by <i>w<sub>i</sub></i>/<i>W<sub>n</sub></i>:\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle {\\begin{aligned}A_{0}&amp;=0\\\\A_{k}&amp;=A_{k-1}+{\\frac {w_{k}}{W_{k}}}(x_{k}-A_{k-1})\\\\Q_{0}&amp;=0\\\\Q_{k}&amp;=Q_{k-1}+{\\frac {w_{k}W_{k-1}}{W_{k}}}(x_{k}-A_{k-1})^{2}=Q_{k-1}+w_{k}(x_{k}-A_{k-1})(x_{k}-A_{k})\\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mtable columnalign="right left right left right left right left right left right left" columnspacing="0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em 2em 0em" displaystyle="true" rowspacing="3pt">\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<msub>\n<mi>A</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mn>0</mn>\n</mtd>\n</mtr>\n<mtr>\n<mtd>\n<msub>\n<mi>A</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mtd>\n<mtd>\n<mi></mi>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>A</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>+</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<msub>\n<mi>w</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<msub>\n<mi>W</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n<msub>\n<mi>x</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>k</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; margin-bottom: -0.273ex; width:72.291ex; height:17.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>In the final division,\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{W_{n}}}\\,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msubsup>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<msub>\n<mi>Q</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<msub>\n<mi>W</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\sigma _{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{W_{n}}}\\,}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="\\sigma _{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{W_{n}}}\\," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/553781109fa6128728b56b102a40561bae707065" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:10.28ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>and\n</p>\n<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\\displaystyle s_{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{W_{n}-1}},}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">\n<semantics>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n<msubsup>\n<mi>s</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>=</mo>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mfrac>\n<msub>\n<mi>Q</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mrow>\n<msub>\n<mi>W</mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n</msub>\n<mo>&#8722;<!-- &#8722; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<mo>,</mo>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle s_{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{W_{n}-1}},}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle s_{n}^{2}={\\frac {Q_{n}}{W_{n}-1}},}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7eddbd55f592ba7778482b66c5b3c8a9409f7482" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; --></mo>\n<mn>1</mn>\n</mrow>\n</mfrac>\n</mrow>\n<msubsup>\n<mi>&#963;<!-- &#963; --></mi>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mi>n</mi>\n</mrow>\n<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n<mn>2</mn>\n</mrow>\n</msubsup>\n<mo>,</mo>\n</mstyle>\n</mrow>\n<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle s_{n}^{2}={\\frac {n\'}{n\'-1}}\\sigma _{n}^{2},}</annotation>\n</semantics>\n</math></span><img alt="{\\displaystyle s_{n}^{2}={\\frac {n\'}{n\'-1}}\\sigma _{n}^{2},}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2252c1ccab0802525b0c7caea0cafa69aad92a51" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:15.518ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>\n<p>where <i>n</i> is the total number of elements, and <i>n\'</i> is the number of elements with non-zero weights.\nThe above formulas become equal to the simpler formulas given above if weights are taken as equal to one.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Standard_deviation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The term <i>standard deviation</i> was first used<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> in writing by <a href="/wiki/Karl_Pearson" title="Karl Pearson">Karl Pearson</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> in 1894, following his use of it in lectures. This was as a replacement for earlier alternative names for the same idea: for example, <a href="/wiki/Carl_Friedrich_Gauss" title="Carl Friedrich Gauss">Gauss</a> used <i>mean error</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span
